BPF0439 ED. 12 23                                          QB814260                                              Page 3

# Page 5

                                                                                          BUSINESSOWNERS
                                                                                       BPF0462 ED. 12 23

                                  EQUIPMENT BREAKDOWN COVERAGE

Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy
carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.

This form modifies insurance provided under the Businessowners
Coverage Form. It applies only when the form number and edition are
shown in the forms schedule or in an endorsement attached to this
policy.

The Declarations and schedules identify the premises, coverage, limit,
deductible, valuation entry, rating basis and premium associated with
this form.

SECTION I - SCHEDULED COVERAGE

A. Coverage Grant
We will provide equipment breakdown only to the extent the coverage is
   shown in the Declarations or schedules and is not excluded or
   limited by this form.
   a. The scheduled coverage, premises reference, form number and
      effective date must be read together.
   b. A coverage summary, certificate, invoice or producer request does
      not broaden coverage or change the applicable limit.

B. Limits And Deductibles
The most we will pay is the applicable limit shown for the scheduled
   coverage. A sublimit shown in this form or an endorsement is part of,
   and does not increase, that limit.
   a. The deductible applies separately to each covered loss unless the
      Declarations or endorsement states another method.
   b. If more than one deductible could apply, the more specific
      deductible for the affected cause of loss or premises controls.

C. Conditions
You must maintain records supporting values, occupancy, payroll, sales,
   contracts, leases, equipment, operations and other rating information
   used to issue this form.
At our request, you must allow inspection of the described premises and
   must provide books and records needed for audit, claim review or
   policy correction.

D. Valuation And Period Of Coverage
Valuation, waiting periods, restoration periods and other time-based
   provisions are determined by the Declarations and by the schedule
   that names this form.
If the Declarations show a valuation basis or time period for the
   scheduled coverage, that entry applies only to the premises to which
   the form is attached.

SECTION II - EXCLUSIONS AND LIMITATIONS
We do not pay for loss, cost or liability excluded by the Businessowners
Coverage Form, by this form, or by any endorsement effective for the
same scheduled coverage.
   a. No coverage is provided unless it is described by the applicable
      schedule, form number and premises reference.
   b. No oral statement, binder note, certificate, finance agreement or
      billing notice changes this form.
   c. If this form applies to more than one scheduled premises, each
      premises is treated separately for limits, deductibles and
      conditions unless the schedule states otherwise.

SECTION III - CHANGES TO THIS FORM
Any change to this form must be made by endorsement issued by us. If
two endorsements conflict, the endorsement with the later effective date
controls for the affected coverage.
A change in ownership, occupancy, use, operations or rating basis must
be reported as required by the Common Policy Conditions and any state
amendatory endorsement.

SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ
Coverage for equipment breakdown is determined by reading the
Declarations, this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement
naming the same coverage and premises reference.
If the same coverage appears on multiple schedules, use the location,
building, form number and effective date to connect the entries.


BPF0462 ED. 12 23                                            QB814260                                            Page 4

# Page 6

                                                                                BUSINESSOWNERS
                                                                                BPF1518 ED. 06 21

                           EMPLOYEE DISHONESTY OPTIONAL COVERAGE

Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy
carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.

This form modifies insurance provided under the Businessowners
Coverage Form. It applies only when the form number and edition are
shown in the forms schedule or in an endorsement attached to this
policy.

The Declarations and schedules identify the premises, coverage, limit,
deductible, valuation entry, rating basis and premium associated with
this form.

SECTION I - SCHEDULED COVERAGE

A. Coverage Grant
We will provide employee dishonesty only to the extent the coverage is
shown in the Declarations or schedules and is not excluded or
limited by this form.

  a. The scheduled coverage, premises reference, form number and
     effective date must be read together.

  b. A coverage summary, certificate, invoice or producer request does
     not broaden coverage or change the applicable limit.

B. Limits And Deductibles
The most we will pay is the applicable limit shown for the scheduled
coverage. A sublimit shown in this form or an endorsement is part of,
and does not increase, that limit.

  a. The deductible applies separately to each covered loss unless the
     Declarations or endorsement states another method.

  b. If more than one deductible could apply, the more specific
     deductible for the affected cause of loss or premises controls.

C. Conditions
You must maintain records supporting values, occupancy, payroll, sales,
contracts, leases, equipment, operations and other rating information
used to issue this form.

At our request, you must allow inspection of the described premises and
must provide books and records needed for audit, claim review or
policy correction.

D. Valuation And Period Of Coverage
Valuation, waiting periods, restoration periods and other time-based
provisions are determined by the Declarations and by the schedule
that names this form.

If the Declarations show a valuation basis or time period for the
scheduled coverage, that entry applies only to the premises to which
the form is attached.

SECTION II - EXCLUSIONS AND LIMITATIONS
We do not pay for loss, cost or liability excluded by the Businessowners
Coverage Form, by this form, or by any endorsement effective for the
same scheduled coverage.

  a. No coverage is provided unless it is described by the applicable
     schedule, form number and premises reference.

  b. No oral statement, binder note, certificate, finance agreement or
     billing notice changes this form.

  c. If this form applies to more than one scheduled premises, each
     premises is treated separately for limits, deductibles and
     conditions unless the schedule states otherwise.

SECTION III - CHANGES TO THIS FORM
Any change to this form must be made by endorsement issued by us. If
two endorsements conflict, the endorsement with the later effective date
controls for the affected coverage.

A change in ownership, occupancy, use, operations or rating basis must
be reported as required by the Common Policy Conditions and any state
amendatory endorsement.

SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ
Coverage for employee dishonesty is determined by reading the
Declarations, this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement
naming the same coverage and premises reference.

If the same coverage appears on multiple schedules, use the location,
building, form number and effective date to connect the entries.

                            POLICYHOLDER NOTICE
==============================================================================

THIS NOTICE IS PROVIDED FOR INFORMATIONAL PURPOSES.
IT DOES NOT CHANGE THE COVERAGE PROVIDED BY THIS POLICY.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

NOTICE TO POLICYHOLDER

The policy consists of the declarations, coverage forms, schedules, notices,
and endorsements issued by the company. Read all pages together before
relying on a single schedule or summary.

A certificate of insurance, billing statement, producer correspondence,
or claim notice does not change a limit, deductible, location, form,
classification, exclusion, premium, or effective date.

If the policyholder requests a change, the change is effective only when
the company issues an endorsement or revised declarations page. Retain
all later endorsements with the policy packet.

Questions about billing, audit, loss reporting, or policy changes should
be directed to the producer or servicing office shown in the declarations.

The forms schedule identifies the edition date for each coverage form,
endorsement, amendatory page and notice attached to the policy packet.

If more than one schedule refers to the same location or building, read
the location number, building number, coverage name, form number, and
effective date together before relying on the entry.

The insured should retain the full packet, including replaced pages,
because later endorsements may apply only from their effective dates.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

KEEP THIS NOTICE WITH YOUR POLICY FOR FUTURE REFERENCE.

ACCOUNT SUMMARY
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
POLICY NUMBER: QB814260                       BILLING METHOD: DIRECT BILL
NAMED INSURED: Pinecrest Print Cooperative, LLC
SCHEDULED COVERAGE: Outdoor Property
LOCATION: 001 BUILDING: 002 SCHEDULED PREMIUM:       $418
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PREMIUM CONDITIONS

1. Premium shown in this policy is an estimate unless the declarations or
   premium schedule states that the premium is fully earned or not auditable.

2. Final premium may depend on payroll, sales, property values, occupancy,
   location, classification, endorsements, and other rating information.

3. The insured must keep records needed to verify the premium basis and
   must make those records available for audit during normal business hours.

4. A payment plan, installment bill, finance agreement, or invoice does not
   amend coverage and does not replace the declarations or schedules.

5. Return premium, additional premium, fees, and taxes are calculated using
   the policy terms, rating plan, and applicable law.

6. Premium shown for a single scheduled coverage does not change limits,
   deductibles, valuation terms, covered premises, or exclusions.

7. If the insured requests a change during the policy period, any resulting
   premium adjustment applies from the effective date shown on the
   endorsement or revised declarations page.

8. Audit correspondence, worksheets, and installment notices are part of
   policy administration records and should be retained with this packet.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
THIS PAGE IS PART OF THE POLICY PACKET BUT DOES NOT GRANT COVERAGE.

                               POLICYHOLDER NOTICE
================================================================================

THIS NOTICE IS PROVIDED FOR INFORMATIONAL PURPOSES.
IT DOES NOT CHANGE THE COVERAGE PROVIDED BY THIS POLICY.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

NOTICE TO POLICYHOLDER

The policy consists of the declarations, coverage forms, schedules, notices,
and endorsements issued by the company. Read all pages together before
relying on a single schedule or summary.

A certificate of insurance, billing statement, producer correspondence,
or claim notice does not change a limit, deductible, location, form,
classification, exclusion, premium, or effective date.

If the policyholder requests a change, the change is effective only when
the company issues an endorsement or revised declarations page. Retain
all later endorsements with the policy packet.

Questions about billing, audit, loss reporting, or policy changes should
be directed to the producer or servicing office shown in the declarations.

The forms schedule identifies the edition date for each coverage form,
endorsement, amendatory page and notice attached to the policy packet.

If more than one schedule refers to the same location or building, read
the location number, building number, coverage name, form number, and
effective date together before relying on the entry.

The insured should retain the full packet, including replaced pages,
because later endorsements may apply only from their effective dates.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
KEEP THIS NOTICE WITH YOUR POLICY FOR FUTURE REFERENCE.

BUSINESSOWNERS
BPF0013 ED. 01 20

# BUSINESSOWNERS COVERAGE FORM

Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.

Throughout this Coverage Form, the words "you" and "your" refer to the Named Insured shown in the Declarations. The words "we", "us" and "our" refer to the company providing this insurance.

Other words and phrases that appear in quotation marks have special meaning. Refer to the Definitions section and to any endorsement that changes this form.

### SECTION I - PROPERTY

**A. Coverage**
We will pay for direct physical loss of or damage to Covered Property at the premises described in the Declarations caused by or resulting from a Covered Cause of Loss.

**1. Covered Property**
Covered Property includes Buildings as described under Paragraph a. below, Business Personal Property as described under Paragraph b. below, or both, depending on whether a Limit Of Insurance is shown in the Declarations.

  a. Buildings, meaning the buildings and structures at the described premises, including:
     (1) Completed additions;
     (2) Fixtures, including outdoor fixtures;
     (3) Permanently installed machinery and equipment; and
     (4) Personal property owned by you that is used to maintain or service the buildings or structures or the premises.

  b. Business Personal Property located in or on the buildings at the described premises, or in the open or in a vehicle within 100 feet of those premises, including:
     (1) Property you own that is used in your business;
     (2) Property of others that is in your care, custody or control, except as otherwise provided in this policy; and
     (3) Tenant improvements and betterments made a part of a building or structure you occupy but do not own.

**2. Property Not Covered**
Covered Property does not include aircraft, watercraft, automobiles, money, securities, contraband, land, crops, lawns, outdoor fences, electronic data, or any property more specifically excluded by this form or by endorsement.

**3. Covered Causes Of Loss**
Direct physical loss is covered unless the loss is excluded or limited in this Coverage Form or in an endorsement attached to this policy.

**4. Limitations**
We will not pay for loss of or damage to property that is missing where the only evidence of loss is an inventory shortage, unexplained disappearance, or shortage disclosed on taking inventory.

### SECTION II - ADDITIONAL COVERAGES

Additional coverages apply only within the limit, period, territory and conditions stated for the coverage. These coverages do not increase the Limits Of Insurance unless this form or an endorsement specifically states otherwise.

  a. Debris removal, preservation of property, fire department service charge and related expenses are subject to the terms shown in the Declarations and schedules.

  b. Business income, extra expense and ordinary payroll provisions require records showing sales, payroll, continuing expenses and the period of restoration.

### SECTION III - CONDITIONS

The following conditions apply in addition to the Common Policy Conditions and any conditions shown in the Declarations or endorsements.

  a. You must give prompt notice of loss, protect covered property from further damage, and keep an accurate record of repair costs and emergency expenses.

  b. At our request, you must provide inventories, invoices, lease agreements, payroll records, sales records, diagrams and other records supporting the claim.

  c. If another form or endorsement addresses the same subject, the more specific provision controls for the affected coverage.

### SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ

Coverage for building is determined by reading the Declarations, this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement naming the same coverage and premises reference.

If a schedule and an endorsement both refer to the same coverage and premises, use the later effective date and the more specific policy provision.

                      PREMIUM AUDIT AND ACCOUNTING CONDITIONS
================================================================================

ACCOUNT SUMMARY
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
POLICY NUMBER: QB814260               BILLING METHOD: DIRECT BILL
NAMED INSURED: Pinecrest Print Cooperative, LLC
SCHEDULED COVERAGE: Business Income and Extra Expense
LOCATION: 001 BUILDING: 002 SCHEDULED PREMIUM:        $650
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PREMIUM CONDITIONS

1. Premium shown in this policy is an estimate unless the declarations or
   premium schedule states that the premium is fully earned or not auditable.

2. Final premium may depend on payroll, sales, property values, occupancy,
   location, classification, endorsements, and other rating information.

3. The insured must keep records needed to verify the premium basis and
   must make those records available for audit during normal business hours.

4. A payment plan, installment bill, finance agreement, or invoice does not
   amend coverage and does not replace the declarations or schedules.

5. Return premium, additional premium, fees, and taxes are calculated using
   the policy terms, rating plan, and applicable law.

6. Premium shown for a single scheduled coverage does not change limits,
   deductibles, valuation terms, covered premises, or exclusions.

7. If the insured requests a change during the policy period, any resulting
   premium adjustment applies from the effective date shown on the
   endorsement or revised declarations page.

8. Audit correspondence, worksheets, and installment notices are part of
   policy administration records and should be retained with this packet.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BPF1518 ED. 06 21

# EMPLOYEE DISHONESTY OPTIONAL COVERAGE

Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.

This form modifies insurance provided under the Businessowners Coverage Form. It applies only when the form number and edition are shown in the forms schedule or in an endorsement attached to this policy.

The Declarations and schedules identify the premises, coverage, limit, deductible, valuation entry, rating basis and premium associated with this form.

### SECTION I - SCHEDULED COVERAGE

**A. Coverage Grant**
We will provide employee dishonesty only to the extent the coverage is shown in the Declarations or schedules and is not excluded or limited by this form.

a. The scheduled coverage, premises reference, form number and effective date must be read together.
b. A coverage summary, certificate, invoice or producer request does not broaden coverage or change the applicable limit.

**B. Limits And Deductibles**
The most we will pay is the applicable limit shown for the scheduled coverage. A sublimit shown in this form or an endorsement is part of, and does not increase, that limit.

a. The deductible applies separately to each covered loss unless the Declarations or endorsement states another method.
b. If more than one deductible could apply, the more specific deductible for the affected cause of loss or premises controls.

**C. Conditions**
You must maintain records supporting values, occupancy, payroll, sales, contracts, leases, equipment, operations and other rating information used to issue this form.

At our request, you must allow inspection of the described premises and must provide books and records needed for audit, claim review or policy correction.

**D. Valuation And Period Of Coverage**
Valuation, waiting periods, restoration periods and other time-based provisions are determined by the Declarations and by the schedule that names this form.

If the Declarations show a valuation basis or time period for the scheduled coverage, that entry applies only to the premises to which the form is attached.

### SECTION II - EXCLUSIONS AND LIMITATIONS
We do not pay for loss, cost or liability excluded by the Businessowners Coverage Form, by this form, or by any endorsement effective for the same scheduled coverage.

a. No coverage is provided unless it is described by the applicable schedule, form number and premises reference.
b. No oral statement, binder note, certificate, finance agreement or billing notice changes this form.
c. If this form applies to more than one scheduled premises, each premises is treated separately for limits, deductibles and conditions unless the schedule states otherwise.

### SECTION III - CHANGES TO THIS FORM
Any change to this form must be made by endorsement issued by us. If two endorsements conflict, the endorsement with the later effective date controls for the affected coverage.

A change in ownership, occupancy, use, operations or rating basis must be reported as required by the Common Policy Conditions and any state amendatory endorsement.

### SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ
Coverage for employee dishonesty is determined by reading the Declarations, this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement naming the same coverage and premises reference.

If the same coverage appears on multiple schedules, use the location, building, form number and effective date to connect the entries.

***

SCHEDULE
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
APPLIES IN: NH          POLICY FORM: BUSINESSOWNERS COVERAGE FORM
LOCATION: 001 BUILDING: 002 FORM REFERENCE: BPF 04 28
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following provisions amend the policy only to the extent required by
law or regulation applicable to the state shown in the schedule.

1. Cancellation, nonrenewal, and conditional renewal notices are provided
   according to the time period required by applicable law.

2. Any provision conflicting with mandatory state law is amended to conform
   to that law, but only for the policy or premises subject to that law.

3. Duties after loss, appraisal, legal action, and proof-of-loss provisions
   apply as amended by this endorsement and the declarations.

4. This endorsement does not change scheduled limits, deductibles, forms,
   classifications, rating bases, or premiums unless a row in the schedule
   or another endorsement specifically states the change.

5. If this endorsement conflicts with another state amendatory endorsement,
   the provision applicable to the described premises controls.

6. Notice periods, appraisal rights, cancellation terms, and suit limitation
   provisions apply only as amended for the state and policy period shown.

7. This endorsement must be read with the declarations, coverage form,
   forms schedule, and any endorsement naming the same location or coverage.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
ALL OTHER TERMS AND CONDITIONS OF THIS POLICY REMAIN UNCHANGED.

                     WATER BACK-UP AND SUMP OVERFLOW

Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy
carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.

This form modifies insurance provided under the Businessowners
Coverage Form. It applies only when the form number and edition are
shown in the forms schedule or in an endorsement attached to this
policy.

The Declarations and schedules identify the premises, coverage, limit,
deductible, valuation entry, rating basis and premium associated with
this form.

SECTION I - SCHEDULED COVERAGE

A. Coverage Grant
   We will provide water back-up only to the extent the coverage is shown
   in the Declarations or schedules and is not excluded or limited by
   this form.
   a. The scheduled coverage, premises reference, form number and
      effective date must be read together.
   b. A coverage summary, certificate, invoice or producer request does
      not broaden coverage or change the applicable limit.

B. Limits And Deductibles
   The most we will pay is the applicable limit shown for the scheduled
   coverage. A sublimit shown in this form or an endorsement is part of,
   and does not increase, that limit.
   a. The deductible applies separately to each covered loss unless the
      Declarations or endorsement states another method.
   b. If more than one deductible could apply, the more specific
      deductible for the affected cause of loss or premises controls.

C. Conditions
   You must maintain records supporting values, occupancy, payroll, sales,
   contracts, leases, equipment, operations and other rating information
   used to issue this form.
   At our request, you must allow inspection of the described premises and
   must provide books and records needed for audit, claim review or
   policy correction.

D. Valuation And Period Of Coverage
   Valuation, waiting periods, restoration periods and other time-based
   provisions are determined by the Declarations and by the schedule
   that names this form.
   If the Declarations show a valuation basis or time period for the
   scheduled coverage, that entry applies only to the premises to which
   the form is attached.

SECTION II - EXCLUSIONS AND LIMITATIONS
We do not pay for loss, cost or liability excluded by the Businessowners
Coverage Form, by this form, or by any endorsement effective for the
same scheduled coverage.
a. No coverage is provided unless it is described by the applicable
   schedule, form number and premises reference.
b. No oral statement, binder note, certificate, finance agreement or
   billing notice changes this form.
c. If this form applies to more than one scheduled premises, each
   premises is treated separately for limits, deductibles and
   conditions unless the schedule states otherwise.

SECTION III - CHANGES TO THIS FORM
Any change to this form must be made by endorsement issued by us. If
two endorsements conflict, the endorsement with the later effective date
controls for the affected coverage.
A change in ownership, occupancy, use, operations or rating basis must
be reported as required by the Common Policy Conditions and any state
amendatory endorsement.

SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ
Coverage for water back-up is determined by reading the Declarations,
this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement naming the same
coverage and premises reference.
If the same coverage appears on multiple schedules, use the location,
building, form number and effective date to connect the entries.

PREMIUM CONDITIONS

1. Premium shown in this policy is an estimate unless the declarations or
   premium schedule states that the premium is fully earned or not auditable.

2. Final premium may depend on payroll, sales, property values, occupancy,
   location, classification, endorsements, and other rating information.

3. The insured must keep records needed to verify the premium basis and
   must make those records available for audit during normal business hours.

4. A payment plan, installment bill, finance agreement, or invoice does not
   amend coverage and does not replace the declarations or schedules.

5. Return premium, additional premium, fees, and taxes are calculated using
   the policy terms, rating plan, and applicable law.

6. Premium shown for a single scheduled coverage does not change limits,
   deductibles, valuation terms, covered premises, or exclusions.

7. If the insured requests a change during the policy period, any resulting
   premium adjustment applies from the effective date shown on the
   endorsement or revised declarations page.

8. Audit correspondence, worksheets, and installment notices are part of
   policy administration records and should be retained with this packet.

APPLIES IN: NH          POLICY FORM: BUSINESSOWNERS COVERAGE FORM

The following provisions amend the policy only to the extent required by
law or regulation applicable to the state shown in the schedule.

1. Cancellation, nonrenewal, and conditional renewal notices are provided
   according to the time period required by applicable law.

2. Any provision conflicting with mandatory state law is amended to conform
   to that law, but only for the policy or premises subject to that law.

3. Duties after loss, appraisal, legal action, and proof-of-loss provisions
   apply as amended by this endorsement and the declarations.

4. This endorsement does not change scheduled limits, deductibles, forms,
   classifications, rating bases, or premiums unless a row in the schedule
   or another endorsement specifically states the change.

5. If this endorsement conflicts with another state amendatory endorsement,
   the provision applicable to the described premises controls.

6. Notice periods, appraisal rights, cancellation terms, and suit limitation
   provisions apply only as amended for the state and policy period shown.

7. This endorsement must be read with the declarations, coverage form,
   forms schedule, and any endorsement naming the same location or coverage.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
ALL OTHER TERMS AND CONDITIONS OF THIS POLICY REMAIN UNCHANGED.

                               POLICYHOLDER NOTICE
================================================================================

THIS NOTICE IS PROVIDED FOR INFORMATIONAL PURPOSES.
IT DOES NOT CHANGE THE COVERAGE PROVIDED BY THIS POLICY.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

NOTICE TO POLICYHOLDER

The policy consists of the declarations, coverage forms, schedules, notices,
and endorsements issued by the company. Read all pages together before
relying on a single schedule or summary.

A certificate of insurance, billing statement, producer correspondence,
or claim notice does not change a limit, deductible, location, form,
classification, exclusion, premium, or effective date.

If the policyholder requests a change, the change is effective only when
the company issues an endorsement or revised declarations page. Retain
all later endorsements with the policy packet.

Questions about billing, audit, loss reporting, or policy changes should
be directed to the producer or servicing office shown in the declarations.

The forms schedule identifies the edition date for each coverage form,
endorsement, amendatory page and notice attached to the policy packet.

If more than one schedule refers to the same location or building, read
the location number, building number, coverage name, form number, and
effective date together before relying on the entry.

The insured should retain the full packet, including replaced pages,
because later endorsements may apply only from their effective dates.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
KEEP THIS NOTICE WITH YOUR POLICY FOR FUTURE REFERENCE.

                          EQUIPMENT BREAKDOWN COVERAGE



Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy
carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.

This form modifies insurance provided under the Businessowners
Coverage Form. It applies only when the form number and edition are
shown in the forms schedule or in an endorsement attached to this
policy.

The Declarations and schedules identify the premises, coverage, limit,
deductible, valuation entry, rating basis and premium associated with
this form.

SECTION I - SCHEDULED COVERAGE

A. Coverage Grant
We will provide equipment breakdown only to the extent the coverage is
   shown in the Declarations or schedules and is not excluded or
   limited by this form.
   a. The scheduled coverage, premises reference, form number and
      effective date must be read together.
   b. A coverage summary, certificate, invoice or producer request does
      not broaden coverage or change the applicable limit.

B. Limits And Deductibles
The most we will pay is the applicable limit shown for the scheduled
   coverage. A sublimit shown in this form or an endorsement is part of,
   and does not increase, that limit.
   a. The deductible applies separately to each covered loss unless the
      Declarations or endorsement states another method.
   b. If more than one deductible could apply, the more specific
      deductible for the affected cause of loss or premises controls.

C. Conditions
You must maintain records supporting values, occupancy, payroll, sales,
   contracts, leases, equipment, operations and other rating information
   used to issue this form.

At our request, you must allow inspection of the described premises and
   must provide books and records needed for audit, claim review or
   policy correction.

D. Valuation And Period Of Coverage
Valuation, waiting periods, restoration periods and other time-based
   provisions are determined by the Declarations and by the schedule
   that names this form.

If the Declarations show a valuation basis or time period for the
   scheduled coverage, that entry applies only to the premises to which
   the form is attached.

SECTION II - EXCLUSIONS AND LIMITATIONS
We do not pay for loss, cost or liability excluded by the Businessowners
Coverage Form, by this form, or by any endorsement effective for the
same scheduled coverage.
   a. No coverage is provided unless it is described by the applicable
      schedule, form number and premises reference.
   b. No oral statement, binder note, certificate, finance agreement or
      billing notice changes this form.
   c. If this form applies to more than one scheduled premises, each
      premises is treated separately for limits, deductibles and
      conditions unless the schedule states otherwise.

SECTION III - CHANGES TO THIS FORM
Any change to this form must be made by endorsement issued by us. If
two endorsements conflict, the endorsement with the later effective date
controls for the affected coverage.

A change in ownership, occupancy, use, operations or rating basis must
be reported as required by the Common Policy Conditions and any state
amendatory endorsement.

SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ
Coverage for equipment breakdown is determined by reading the
Declarations, this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement
naming the same coverage and premises reference.

If the same coverage appears on multiple schedules, use the location,
building, form number and effective date to connect the entries.

                               POLICYHOLDER NOTICE
=============================================================================

THIS NOTICE IS PROVIDED FOR INFORMATIONAL PURPOSES.
IT DOES NOT CHANGE THE COVERAGE PROVIDED BY THIS POLICY.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

NOTICE TO POLICYHOLDER

The policy consists of the declarations, coverage forms, schedules, notices,
and endorsements issued by the company. Read all pages together before
relying on a single schedule or summary.

A certificate of insurance, billing statement, producer correspondence,
or claim notice does not change a limit, deductible, location, form,
classification, exclusion, premium, or effective date.

If the policyholder requests a change, the change is effective only when
the company issues an endorsement or revised declarations page. Retain
all later endorsements with the policy packet.

Questions about billing, audit, loss reporting, or policy changes should
be directed to the producer or servicing office shown in the declarations.

The forms schedule identifies the edition date for each coverage form,
endorsement, amendatory page and notice attached to the policy packet.

If more than one schedule refers to the same location or building, read
the location number, building number, coverage name, form number, and
effective date together before relying on the entry.

The insured should retain the full packet, including replaced pages,
because later endorsements may apply only from their effective dates.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
KEEP THIS NOTICE WITH YOUR POLICY FOR FUTURE REFERENCE.

                                                                         BPF0491 ED. 01 20

                       WATER BACK-UP AND SUMP OVERFLOW

Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy
carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.

This form modifies insurance provided under the Businessowners
Coverage Form. It applies only when the form number and edition are
shown in the forms schedule or in an endorsement attached to this
policy.

The Declarations and schedules identify the premises, coverage, limit,
deductible, valuation entry, rating basis and premium associated with
this form.

SECTION I - SCHEDULED COVERAGE

A. Coverage Grant
   We will provide water back-up only to the extent the coverage is shown
   in the Declarations or schedules and is not excluded or limited by
   this form.
   a. The scheduled coverage, premises reference, form number and
      effective date must be read together.
   b. A coverage summary, certificate, invoice or producer request does
      not broaden coverage or change the applicable limit.

B. Limits And Deductibles
   The most we will pay is the applicable limit shown for the scheduled
   coverage. A sublimit shown in this form or an endorsement is part of,
   and does not increase, that limit.
   a. The deductible applies separately to each covered loss unless the
      Declarations or endorsement states another method.
   b. If more than one deductible could apply, the more specific
      deductible for the affected cause of loss or premises controls.

C. Conditions
   You must maintain records supporting values, occupancy, payroll, sales,
   contracts, leases, equipment, operations and other rating information
   used to issue this form.
   At our request, you must allow inspection of the described premises and
   must provide books and records needed for audit, claim review or
   policy correction.

D. Valuation And Period Of Coverage
   Valuation, waiting periods, restoration periods and other time-based
   provisions are determined by the Declarations and by the schedule
   that names this form.
   If the Declarations show a valuation basis or time period for the
   scheduled coverage, that entry applies only to the premises to which
   the form is attached.

SECTION II - EXCLUSIONS AND LIMITATIONS
   We do not pay for loss, cost or liability excluded by the Businessowners
   Coverage Form, by this form, or by any endorsement effective for the
   same scheduled coverage.
   a. No coverage is provided unless it is described by the applicable
      schedule, form number and premises reference.
   b. No oral statement, binder note, certificate, finance agreement or
      billing notice changes this form.
   c. If this form applies to more than one scheduled premises, each
      premises is treated separately for limits, deductibles and
      conditions unless the schedule states otherwise.

SECTION III - CHANGES TO THIS FORM
   Any change to this form must be made by endorsement issued by us. If
   two endorsements conflict, the endorsement with the later effective date
   controls for the affected coverage.
   A change in ownership, occupancy, use, operations or rating basis must
   be reported as required by the Common Policy Conditions and any state
   amendatory endorsement.

SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ
   Coverage for water back-up is determined by reading the Declarations,
   this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement naming the same
   coverage and premises reference.
   If the same coverage appears on multiple schedules, use the location,
   building, form number and effective date to connect the entries.

# HIRED AUTO AND NON-OWNED AUTO LIABILITY

Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy
carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.

This form modifies insurance provided under the Businessowners
Coverage Form. It applies only when the form number and edition are
shown in the forms schedule or in an endorsement attached to this
policy.

The Declarations and schedules identify the premises, coverage, limit,
deductible, valuation entry, rating basis and premium associated with
this form.

### SECTION I - SCHEDULED COVERAGE

**A. Coverage Grant**
   We will provide hired and non-owned auto only to the extent the
   coverage is shown in the Declarations or schedules and is not
   excluded or limited by this form.

   a. The scheduled coverage, premises reference, form number and
      effective date must be read together.

   b. A coverage summary, certificate, invoice or producer request does
      not broaden coverage or change the applicable limit.

**B. Limits And Deductibles**
   The most we will pay is the applicable limit shown for the scheduled
   coverage. A sublimit shown in this form or an endorsement is part of,
   and does not increase, that limit.

   a. The deductible applies separately to each covered loss unless the
      Declarations or endorsement states another method.

   b. If more than one deductible could apply, the more specific
      deductible for the affected cause of loss or premises controls.

**C. Conditions**
   You must maintain records supporting values, occupancy, payroll, sales,
   contracts, leases, equipment, operations and other rating information
   used to issue this form.

   At our request, you must allow inspection of the described premises and
   must provide books and records needed for audit, claim review or
   policy correction.

**D. Valuation And Period Of Coverage**
   Valuation, waiting periods, restoration periods and other time-based
   provisions are determined by the Declarations and by the schedule
   that names this form.

   If the Declarations show a valuation basis or time period for the
   scheduled coverage, that entry applies only to the premises to which
   the form is attached.

### SECTION II - EXCLUSIONS AND LIMITATIONS

We do not pay for loss, cost or liability excluded by the Businessowners
Coverage Form, by this form, or by any endorsement effective for the
same scheduled coverage.

   a. No coverage is provided unless it is described by the applicable
      schedule, form number and premises reference.

   b. No oral statement, binder note, certificate, finance agreement or
      billing notice changes this form.

   c. If this form applies to more than one scheduled premises, each
      premises is treated separately for limits, deductibles and
      conditions unless the schedule states otherwise.

### SECTION III - CHANGES TO THIS FORM

Any change to this form must be made by endorsement issued by us. If
two endorsements conflict, the endorsement with the later effective date
controls for the affected coverage.

A change in ownership, occupancy, use, operations or rating basis must
be reported as required by the Common Policy Conditions and any state
amendatory endorsement.

### SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ

Coverage for hired and non-owned auto is determined by reading the
Declarations, this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement
naming the same coverage and premises reference.

If the same coverage appears on multiple schedules, use the location,
building, form number and effective date to connect the entries.

SCHEDULED COVERAGE: PFAS Exclusion
LOCATION: 001 BUILDING: 002 SCHEDULED PREMIUM:        $1,298
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PREMIUM CONDITIONS

1. Premium shown in this policy is an estimate unless the declarations or
   premium schedule states that the premium is fully earned or not auditable.

2. Final premium may depend on payroll, sales, property values, occupancy,
   location, classification, endorsements, and other rating information.

3. The insured must keep records needed to verify the premium basis and
   must make those records available for audit during normal business hours.

4. A payment plan, installment bill, finance agreement, or invoice does not
   amend coverage and does not replace the declarations or schedules.

5. Return premium, additional premium, fees, and taxes are calculated using
   the policy terms, rating plan, and applicable law.

6. Premium shown for a single scheduled coverage does not change limits,
   deductibles, valuation terms, covered premises, or exclusions.

7. If the insured requests a change during the policy period, any resulting
   premium adjustment applies from the effective date shown on the
   endorsement or revised declarations page.

8. Audit correspondence, worksheets, and installment notices are part of
   policy administration records and should be retained with this packet.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# ORDINARY PAYROLL LIMITATION

Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.

This form modifies insurance provided under the Businessowners Coverage Form. It applies only when the form number and edition are shown in the forms schedule or in an endorsement attached to this policy.

The Declarations and schedules identify the premises, coverage, limit, deductible, valuation entry, rating basis and premium associated with this form.

### SECTION I - SCHEDULED COVERAGE

#### A. Coverage Grant
We will provide ordinary payroll limitation only to the extent the coverage is shown in the Declarations or schedules and is not excluded or limited by this form.
    a. The scheduled coverage, premises reference, form number and effective date must be read together.
    b. A coverage summary, certificate, invoice or producer request does not broaden coverage or change the applicable limit.

#### B. Limits And Deductibles
The most we will pay is the applicable limit shown for the scheduled coverage. A sublimit shown in this form or an endorsement is part of, and does not increase, that limit.
    a. The deductible applies separately to each covered loss unless the Declarations or endorsement states another method.
    b. If more than one deductible could apply, the more specific deductible for the affected cause of loss or premises controls.

#### C. Conditions
You must maintain records supporting values, occupancy, payroll, sales, contracts, leases, equipment, operations and other rating information used to issue this form.

At our request, you must allow inspection of the described premises and must provide books and records needed for audit, claim review or policy correction.

#### D. Valuation And Period Of Coverage
Valuation, waiting periods, restoration periods and other time-based provisions are determined by the Declarations and by the schedule that names this form.

If the Declarations show a valuation basis or time period for the scheduled coverage, that entry applies only to the premises to which the form is attached.

### SECTION II - EXCLUSIONS AND LIMITATIONS
We do not pay for loss, cost or liability excluded by the Businessowners Coverage Form, by this form, or by any endorsement effective for the same scheduled coverage.
    a. No coverage is provided unless it is described by the applicable schedule, form number and premises reference.
    b. No oral statement, binder note, certificate, finance agreement or billing notice changes this form.
    c. If this form applies to more than one scheduled premises, each premises is treated separately for limits, deductibles and conditions unless the schedule states otherwise.

### SECTION III - CHANGES TO THIS FORM
Any change to this form must be made by endorsement issued by us. If two endorsements conflict, the endorsement with the later effective date controls for the affected coverage.

A change in ownership, occupancy, use, operations or rating basis must be reported as required by the Common Policy Conditions and any state amendatory endorsement.

### SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ
Coverage for ordinary payroll limitation is determined by reading the Declarations, this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement naming the same coverage and premises reference.

If the same coverage appears on multiple schedules, use the location, building, form number and effective date to connect the entries.

LOCATION: 002 BUILDING: 001 FORM REFERENCE: BPF 00 13
------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following provisions amend the policy only to the extent required by
law or regulation applicable to the state shown in the schedule.

1. Cancellation, nonrenewal, and conditional renewal notices are provided
   according to the time period required by applicable law.

2. Any provision conflicting with mandatory state law is amended to conform
   to that law, but only for the policy or premises subject to that law.

3. Duties after loss, appraisal, legal action, and proof-of-loss provisions
   apply as amended by this endorsement and the declarations.

4. This endorsement does not change scheduled limits, deductibles, forms,
   classifications, rating bases, or premiums unless a row in the schedule
   or another endorsement specifically states the change.

5. If this endorsement conflicts with another state amendatory endorsement,
   the provision applicable to the described premises controls.

6. Notice periods, appraisal rights, cancellation terms, and suit limitation
   provisions apply only as amended for the state and policy period shown.

7. This endorsement must be read with the declarations, coverage form,
   forms schedule, and any endorsement naming the same location or coverage.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
ALL OTHER TERMS AND CONDITIONS OF THIS POLICY REMAIN UNCHANGED.

                                 POLICYHOLDER NOTICE
=============================================================================

THIS NOTICE IS PROVIDED FOR INFORMATIONAL PURPOSES.
IT DOES NOT CHANGE THE COVERAGE PROVIDED BY THIS POLICY.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

NOTICE TO POLICYHOLDER

The policy consists of the declarations, coverage forms, schedules, notices,
and endorsements issued by the company. Read all pages together before
relying on a single schedule or summary.

A certificate of insurance, billing statement, producer correspondence,
or claim notice does not change a limit, deductible, location, form,
classification, exclusion, premium, or effective date.

If the policyholder requests a change, the change is effective only when
the company issues an endorsement or revised declarations page. Retain
all later endorsements with the policy packet.

Questions about billing, audit, loss reporting, or policy changes should
be directed to the producer or servicing office shown in the declarations.

The forms schedule identifies the edition date for each coverage form,
endorsement, amendatory page and notice attached to the policy packet.

If more than one schedule refers to the same location or building, read
the location number, building number, coverage name, form number, and
effective date together before relying on the entry.

The insured should retain the full packet, including replaced pages,
because later endorsements may apply only from their effective dates.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
KEEP THIS NOTICE WITH YOUR POLICY FOR FUTURE REFERENCE.

                            MATERIAL POLICY PROVISIONS
            READ WITH DECLARATIONS, SCHEDULES, FORMS AND ENDORSEMENTS
==============================================================================
The following provisions are part of the current policy packet. Each
entry must be read with the scheduled premises, form number, edition
date, and any endorsement applying to the same coverage.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

001. SCHEDULED PREMISES LIMITATION
     For Location 001, Building 001, Building, read BPF 00 13 edition 12 23
     as the controlling limitation provision.
     This provision applies only to Location 001, Building 001, Building
     when BPF 00 13 edition 12 23 is attached to the policy.

002. LIMIT AND DEDUCTIBLE APPLICATION
     The policy applies the following condition provision under BPF 00 13
     edition 12 23 to Location 001, Building 001, Building.
     The scheduled limit of $60,000 and deductible of $1,000 apply to
     Building at the described premises.

003. VALUATION RECORDS REQUIREMENT
     BPF 00 13 edition 12 23 contains a condition provision for Location
     001, Building 001, Building.
     The insured must keep records supporting the Replacement Cost valuation
     basis, 80% coinsurance entry, and 12 Months business income basis.

004. ENDORSEMENT PRIORITY
     For Location 001, Building 001, Building, read BPF 00 13 edition 12 23
     as the controlling condition provision.
     If schedules conflict for Location 001, Building 001, Building, the
     endorsement or form entry with the later effective date controls the
     affected coverage.

005. SCHEDULED PREMISES LIMITATION
     The policy applies the following limitation provision under BPF 00 13
     edition 06 21 to Location 002, Building 001, Business Personal
     Property.
     This provision applies only to Location 002, Building 001, Business
     Personal Property when BPF 00 13 edition 06 21 is attached to the
     policy.

006. LIMIT AND DEDUCTIBLE APPLICATION
     BPF 00 13 edition 06 21 contains a condition provision for Location
     002, Building 001, Business Personal Property.
     The scheduled limit of $75,000 and deductible of $5,000 apply to
     Business Personal Property at the described premises.

007. VALUATION RECORDS REQUIREMENT
     For Location 002, Building 001, Business Personal Property, read BPF 00
     13 edition 06 21 as the controlling condition provision.
     The insured must keep records supporting the Replacement Cost valuation
     basis, 90% coinsurance entry, and 12 Months business income basis.

008. ENDORSEMENT PRIORITY
     The policy applies the following condition provision under BPF 00 13
     edition 06 21 to Location 002, Building 001, Business Personal
     Property.
     If schedules conflict for Location 002, Building 001, Business Personal
     Property, the endorsement or form entry with the later effective date
     controls the affected coverage.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ARCHIVED OR PRIOR-TERM CLAUSES APPEARING ELSEWHERE DO NOT MODIFY THIS POLICY.

ACCOUNT SUMMARY
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
POLICY NUMBER: QB814260             BILLING METHOD: DIRECT BILL
NAMED INSURED: Pinecrest Print Cooperative, LLC
SCHEDULED COVERAGE: Additional Insured by Contract
LOCATION: 002 BUILDING: 001 SCHEDULED PREMIUM:       $1,652
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PREMIUM CONDITIONS

1. Premium shown in this policy is an estimate unless the declarations or
   premium schedule states that the premium is fully earned or not auditable.

2. Final premium may depend on payroll, sales, property values, occupancy,
   location, classification, endorsements, and other rating information.

3. The insured must keep records needed to verify the premium basis and
   must make those records available for audit during normal business hours.

4. A payment plan, installment bill, finance agreement, or invoice does not
   amend coverage and does not replace the declarations or schedules.

5. Return premium, additional premium, fees, and taxes are calculated using
   the policy terms, rating plan, and applicable law.

6. Premium shown for a single scheduled coverage does not change limits,
   deductibles, valuation terms, covered premises, or exclusions.

7. If the insured requests a change during the policy period, any resulting
   premium adjustment applies from the effective date shown on the
   endorsement or revised declarations page.

8. Audit correspondence, worksheets, and installment notices are part of
   policy administration records and should be retained with this packet.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

                               POLICYHOLDER NOTICE
================================================================================

THIS NOTICE IS PROVIDED FOR INFORMATIONAL PURPOSES.
IT DOES NOT CHANGE THE COVERAGE PROVIDED BY THIS POLICY.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

NOTICE TO POLICYHOLDER

The policy consists of the declarations, coverage forms, schedules, notices,
and endorsements issued by the company. Read all pages together before
relying on a single schedule or summary.

A certificate of insurance, billing statement, producer correspondence,
or claim notice does not change a limit, deductible, location, form,
classification, exclusion, premium, or effective date.

If the policyholder requests a change, the change is effective only when
the company issues an endorsement or revised declarations page. Retain
all later endorsements with the policy packet.

Questions about billing, audit, loss reporting, or policy changes should
be directed to the producer or servicing office shown in the declarations.

The forms schedule identifies the edition date for each coverage form,
endorsement, amendatory page and notice attached to the policy packet.

If more than one schedule refers to the same location or building, read
the location number, building number, coverage name, form number, and
effective date together before relying on the entry.

The insured should retain the full packet, including replaced pages,
because later endorsements may apply only from their effective dates.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
KEEP THIS NOTICE WITH YOUR POLICY FOR FUTURE REFERENCE.

                                                                             BUSINESSOWNERS
                                                                             BPF0462 ED. 12 23

                                 EQUIPMENT BREAKDOWN COVERAGE

Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.

This form modifies insurance provided under the Businessowners Coverage Form. It applies only when the form number and edition are shown in the forms schedule or in an endorsement attached to this policy.

The Declarations and schedules identify the premises, coverage, limit, deductible, valuation entry, rating basis and premium associated with this form.

**SECTION I - SCHEDULED COVERAGE**

**A. Coverage Grant**
We will provide equipment breakdown only to the extent the coverage is shown in the Declarations or schedules and is not excluded or limited by this form.

  a. The scheduled coverage, premises reference, form number and effective date must be read together.

  b. A coverage summary, certificate, invoice or producer request does not broaden coverage or change the applicable limit.

**B. Limits And Deductibles**
The most we will pay is the applicable limit shown for the scheduled coverage. A sublimit shown in this form or an endorsement is part of, and does not increase, that limit.

  a. The deductible applies separately to each covered loss unless the Declarations or endorsement states another method.

  b. If more than one deductible could apply, the more specific deductible for the affected cause of loss or premises controls.

**C. Conditions**
You must maintain records supporting values, occupancy, payroll, sales, contracts, leases, equipment, operations and other rating information used to issue this form.

At our request, you must allow inspection of the described premises and must provide books and records needed for audit, claim review or policy correction.

**D. Valuation And Period Of Coverage**
Valuation, waiting periods, restoration periods and other time-based provisions are determined by the Declarations and by the schedule that names this form.

If the Declarations show a valuation basis or time period for the scheduled coverage, that entry applies only to the premises to which the form is attached.

**SECTION II - EXCLUSIONS AND LIMITATIONS**
We do not pay for loss, cost or liability excluded by the Businessowners Coverage Form, by this form, or by any endorsement effective for the same scheduled coverage.

  a. No coverage is provided unless it is described by the applicable schedule, form number and premises reference.

  b. No oral statement, binder note, certificate, finance agreement or billing notice changes this form.

  c. If this form applies to more than one scheduled premises, each premises is treated separately for limits, deductibles and conditions unless the schedule states otherwise.

**SECTION III - CHANGES TO THIS FORM**
Any change to this form must be made by endorsement issued by us. If two endorsements conflict, the endorsement with the later effective date controls for the affected coverage.

A change in ownership, occupancy, use, operations or rating basis must be reported as required by the Common Policy Conditions and any state amendatory endorsement.

**SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ**
Coverage for equipment breakdown is determined by reading the Declarations, this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement naming the same coverage and premises reference.

If the same coverage appears on multiple schedules, use the location, building, form number and effective date to connect the entries.

Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy

policy.

deductible, valuation entry, rating basis and premium associated with
this form.

SECTION I - SCHEDULED COVERAGE

We will provide water back-up only to the extent the coverage is shown
in the Declarations or schedules and is not excluded or limited by
this form.

  a. The scheduled coverage, premises reference, form number and
     effective date must be read together.

  b. A coverage summary, certificate, invoice or producer request does
     not broaden coverage or change the applicable limit.

B. Limits And Deductibles
The most we will pay is the applicable limit shown for the scheduled
coverage. A sublimit shown in this form or an endorsement is part of,
and does not increase, that limit.

  a. The deductible applies separately to each covered loss unless the
     Declarations or endorsement states another method.

  b. If more than one deductible could apply, the more specific
     deductible for the affected cause of loss or premises controls.

C. Conditions
You must maintain records supporting values, occupancy, payroll, sales,
contracts, leases, equipment, operations and other rating information
used to issue this form.

At our request, you must allow inspection of the described premises and
must provide books and records needed for audit, claim review or
policy correction.

D. Valuation And Period Of Coverage
Valuation, waiting periods, restoration periods and other time-based
provisions are determined by the Declarations and by the schedule
that names this form.

If the Declarations show a valuation basis or time period for the
scheduled coverage, that entry applies only to the premises to which
the form is attached.

SECTION II - EXCLUSIONS AND LIMITATIONS
We do not pay for loss, cost or liability excluded by the Businessowners
Coverage Form, by this form, or by any endorsement effective for the
same scheduled coverage.

  a. No coverage is provided unless it is described by the applicable
     schedule, form number and premises reference.

  b. No oral statement, binder note, certificate, finance agreement or
     billing notice changes this form.

  c. If this form applies to more than one scheduled premises, each
     premises is treated separately for limits, deductibles and
     conditions unless the schedule states otherwise.

SECTION III - CHANGES TO THIS FORM
Any change to this form must be made by endorsement issued by us. If
two endorsements conflict, the endorsement with the later effective date
controls for the affected coverage.

A change in ownership, occupancy, use, operations or rating basis must
be reported as required by the Common Policy Conditions and any state
amendatory endorsement.

SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ

this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement naming the same
coverage and premises reference.

If the same coverage appears on multiple schedules, use the location,
building, form number and effective date to connect the entries.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

NOTICE TO POLICYHOLDER

The policy consists of the declarations, coverage forms, schedules, notices,
and endorsements issued by the company. Read all pages together before
relying on a single schedule or summary.

A certificate of insurance, billing statement, producer correspondence,
or claim notice does not change a limit, deductible, location, form,
classification, exclusion, premium, or effective date.

If the policyholder requests a change, the change is effective only when
the company issues an endorsement or revised declarations page. Retain
all later endorsements with the policy packet.

Questions about billing, audit, loss reporting, or policy changes should
be directed to the producer or servicing office shown in the declarations.

The forms schedule identifies the edition date for each coverage form,
endorsement, amendatory page and notice attached to the policy packet.

If more than one schedule refers to the same location or building, read
the location number, building number, coverage name, form number, and
effective date together before relying on the entry.

The insured should retain the full packet, including replaced pages,
because later endorsements may apply only from their effective dates.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
KEEP THIS NOTICE WITH YOUR POLICY FOR FUTURE REFERENCE.

   differs between schedules, the later and more specific endorsement
   controls for that scheduled item.

   agreements, payroll records, sales records and equipment schedules that
   support the scheduled entry.

   applicable limit.

BUSINESSOWNERS COVERAGE FORM

| :--- | :--- |
| Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.<br><br>Throughout this Coverage Form, the words "you" and "your" refer to the Named Insured shown in the Declarations. The words "we", "us" and "our" refer to the company providing this insurance.<br><br>Other words and phrases that appear in quotation marks have special meaning. Refer to the Definitions section and to any endorsement that changes this form.<br><br>**SECTION I - PROPERTY**<br><br>**A. Coverage**<br>We will pay for direct physical loss of or damage to Covered Property at the premises described in the Declarations caused by or resulting from a Covered Cause of Loss.<br><br>**1. Covered Property**<br>Covered Property includes Buildings as described under Paragraph a. below, Business Personal Property as described under Paragraph b. below, or both, depending on whether a Limit Of Insurance is shown in the Declarations.<br><br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a. Buildings, meaning the buildings and structures at the described premises, including:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(1) Completed additions;<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(2) Fixtures, including outdoor fixtures;<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(3) Permanently installed machinery and equipment; and<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(4) Personal property owned by you that is used to maintain or service the buildings or structures or the premises.<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b. Business Personal Property located in or on the buildings at the described premises, or in the open or in a vehicle within 100 feet of those premises, including:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(1) Property you own that is used in your business;<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(2) Property of others that is in your care, custody or control, except as otherwise provided in this policy; and<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(3) Tenant improvements and betterments made a part of a building or structure you occupy but do not own.<br><br>**2. Property Not Covered**<br>Covered Property does not include aircraft, watercraft, automobiles, money, securities, contraband, land, crops, lawns, outdoor fences, electronic data, or any property more specifically excluded by this form or by endorsement. | **3. Covered Causes Of Loss**<br>Direct physical loss is covered unless the loss is excluded or limited in this Coverage Form or in an endorsement attached to this policy.<br><br>**4. Limitations**<br>We will not pay for loss of or damage to property that is missing where the only evidence of loss is an inventory shortage, unexplained disappearance, or shortage disclosed on taking inventory.<br><br>**SECTION II - ADDITIONAL COVERAGES**<br>Additional coverages apply only within the limit, period, territory and conditions stated for the coverage. These coverages do not increase the Limits Of Insurance unless this form or an endorsement specifically states otherwise.<br><br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a. Debris removal, preservation of property, fire department service charge and related expenses are subject to the terms shown in the Declarations and schedules.<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b. Business income, extra expense and ordinary payroll provisions require records showing sales, payroll, continuing expenses and the period of restoration.<br><br>**SECTION III - CONDITIONS**<br>The following conditions apply in addition to the Common Policy Conditions and any conditions shown in the Declarations or endorsements.<br><br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a. You must give prompt notice of loss, protect covered property from further damage, and keep an accurate record of repair costs and emergency expenses.<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;b. At our request, you must provide inventories, invoices, lease agreements, payroll records, sales records, diagrams and other records supporting the claim.<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;c. If another form or endorsement addresses the same subject, the more specific provision controls for the affected coverage.<br><br>**SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ**<br>Coverage for business personal property is determined by reading the Declarations, this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement naming the same coverage and premises reference.<br><br>If a schedule and an endorsement both refer to the same coverage and premises, use the later effective date and the more specific policy provision. |

                    PREMIUM AUDIT AND ACCOUNTING CONDITIONS
===============================================================================

ACCOUNT SUMMARY
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
POLICY NUMBER: QB814260                 BILLING METHOD: DIRECT BILL
NAMED INSURED: Pinecrest Print Cooperative, LLC
SCHEDULED COVERAGE: Employee Dishonesty
LOCATION: 001 BUILDING: 001 SCHEDULED PREMIUM:        $667
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PREMIUM CONDITIONS

1. Premium shown in this policy is an estimate unless the declarations or
   premium schedule states that the premium is fully earned or not auditable.

2. Final premium may depend on payroll, sales, property values, occupancy,
   location, classification, endorsements, and other rating information.

3. The insured must keep records needed to verify the premium basis and
   must make those records available for audit during normal business hours.

4. A payment plan, installment bill, finance agreement, or invoice does not
   amend coverage and does not replace the declarations or schedules.

5. Return premium, additional premium, fees, and taxes are calculated using
   the policy terms, rating plan, and applicable law.

6. Premium shown for a single scheduled coverage does not change limits,
   deductibles, valuation terms, covered premises, or exclusions.

7. If the insured requests a change during the policy period, any resulting
   premium adjustment applies from the effective date shown on the
   endorsement or revised declarations page.

8. Audit correspondence, worksheets, and installment notices are part of
   policy administration records and should be retained with this packet.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
THIS PAGE IS PART OF THE POLICY PACKET BUT DOES NOT GRANT COVERAGE.

PREMIUM CONDITIONS

1. Premium shown in this policy is an estimate unless the declarations or
   premium schedule states that the premium is fully earned or not auditable.

2. Final premium may depend on payroll, sales, property values, occupancy,
   location, classification, endorsements, and other rating information.

3. The insured must keep records needed to verify the premium basis and
   must make those records available for audit during normal business hours.

4. A payment plan, installment bill, finance agreement, or invoice does not
   amend coverage and does not replace the declarations or schedules.

5. Return premium, additional premium, fees, and taxes are calculated using
   the policy terms, rating plan, and applicable law.

6. Premium shown for a single scheduled coverage does not change limits,
   deductibles, valuation terms, covered premises, or exclusions.

7. If the insured requests a change during the policy period, any resulting
   premium adjustment applies from the effective date shown on the
   endorsement or revised declarations page.

8. Audit correspondence, worksheets, and installment notices are part of
   policy administration records and should be retained with this packet.

                         ORDINARY PAYROLL LIMITATION

Various provisions in this policy restrict coverage. Read the entire policy
carefully to determine rights, duties and what is and is not covered.

This form modifies insurance provided under the Businessowners
Coverage Form. It applies only when the form number and edition are
shown in the forms schedule or in an endorsement attached to this
policy.

The Declarations and schedules identify the premises, coverage, limit,
deductible, valuation entry, rating basis and premium associated with
this form.

SECTION I - SCHEDULED COVERAGE

A. Coverage Grant
We will provide ordinary payroll limitation only to the extent the coverage
is shown in the Declarations or schedules and is not excluded or
limited by this form.
    a. The scheduled coverage, premises reference, form number and
       effective date must be read together.
    b. A coverage summary, certificate, invoice or producer request does
       not broaden coverage or change the applicable limit.

B. Limits And Deductibles
The most we will pay is the applicable limit shown for the scheduled
coverage. A sublimit shown in this form or an endorsement is part of,
and does not increase, that limit.
    a. The deductible applies separately to each covered loss unless the
       Declarations or endorsement states another method.
    b. If more than one deductible could apply, the more specific
       deductible for the affected cause of loss or premises controls.

C. Conditions
You must maintain records supporting values, occupancy, payroll, sales,
contracts, leases, equipment, operations and other rating information
used to issue this form.
At our request, you must allow inspection of the described premises and
must provide books and records needed for audit, claim review or
policy correction.

D. Valuation And Period Of Coverage
Valuation, waiting periods, restoration periods and other time-based
provisions are determined by the Declarations and by the schedule
that names this form.
If the Declarations show a valuation basis or time period for the
scheduled coverage, that entry applies only to the premises to which
the form is attached.

SECTION II - EXCLUSIONS AND LIMITATIONS
We do not pay for loss, cost or liability excluded by the Businessowners
Coverage Form, by this form, or by any endorsement effective for the
same scheduled coverage.
    a. No coverage is provided unless it is described by the applicable
       schedule, form number and premises reference.
    b. No oral statement, binder note, certificate, finance agreement or
       billing notice changes this form.
    c. If this form applies to more than one scheduled premises, each
       premises is treated separately for limits, deductibles and
       conditions unless the schedule states otherwise.

SECTION III - CHANGES TO THIS FORM
Any change to this form must be made by endorsement issued by us. If
two endorsements conflict, the endorsement with the later effective date
controls for the affected coverage.
A change in ownership, occupancy, use, operations or rating basis must
be reported as required by the Common Policy Conditions and any state
amendatory endorsement.

SECTION IV - HOW THIS FORM IS READ
Coverage for ordinary payroll limitation is determined by reading the
Declarations, this form, the forms schedule and any endorsement
naming the same coverage and premises reference.
If the same coverage appears on multiple schedules, use the location,
building, form number and effective date to connect the entries.
